 The deputy commissioners there (deputy Commissioners) have given a clean chit to Vadra, denying any wrongdoing
 inspector general of registration ko bheji apni report main gudgaanv, faridabad, mevaat or palaval ke dipti kamishnaron ne kaha he ki jameenon kii kharid main koi aniyamitata nahin barti gai, jameen saudon kii registry sarkari cirkil rate ke mutabik hui, or in sabhi saudon main stamp duty kaa puraa bhugtan kiya gaya he, isliye inamen rajasav kii koi haani nahin hui
 According to the report of Mewat deputy commissioner Wazir Singh Goyat, no disturbance has been found in the six registries of 29 acres of land Vadra bought in Shikarpuri village
 palaval ke dipti kamishnar vijay dahia kii report ke mutabik hasanpur gaanv main kharidi gai 74 acre jameen kii keemat kam nahin aanki gai or stamp duty bhi cirkil rate ke hisaab se hi chukaai gai he
 According to Gurgaon Deputy Commissioner PC Meena, there is no flaw in the 47-acre land deal between Vadra and DLF in Shikohpur village
 tippaniyan Farizabad deputy commissioner Balraj Singh's report said that in 11 registrations of 52 acres of land attached to Vadra, no such thing has been found in the lower price of the land
 kaha ja rahaa he ki dipti kamishnaron kii in anukool reporton ke baad us jaanch cameti kaa kaam kaaphi aasaan ho jayega, jo ashok khemka ke adeshon kii jaanch ke liye gathit kii gai thi
 It is noteworthy that before Khemka took over after the transfer, the cancellation of the dismissal of three and a half acres sold to DLF by Robert Vadra's company Skylight, along with the deputies of Mewat, Palwal, Faridabad and Gurgaon The commissioners had ordered an inquiry into all the land purchased by Vadra
 ab khemka ke in adeshon kii jaanch ek teen-sadasyeey cameti kar rahi he
 In their report sent to the Inspector General of Registration, deputy commissioners of Gurgaon, Faridabad, Mewat and Palwal have said that no irregularities were observed in the purchase of land, the registration of land deals was done according to the government circle rate, and all these deals were stamped
 Duty has been paid in full, so there was no loss of revenue in them
 mevaat ke dipti kamishnar vajeer singh goyat kii report ke anusaar shikarpuri gaanv main wadra ne jo 29 acre jameen kharidi, uski chah registrion main koi gadabadi nahin pai gai he
 According to the report of Palwal deputy commissioner Vijay Dahiya, the price of 74 acres of land purchased in Hasanpur village has not been reduced and stamp duty has also been paid at the circle rate
 gudgaanv ke dipti kamishnar pisi meena ke anusaar shikohpur gaanv main wadra or dlef ke bich hue 47 acre jameen ke saude main bhi koi khami nahin pai gai he

 However, the mileage of any vehicle depends on the power of its engine
 lekin kuch aise tips hai jisaki madad se aap apane car kii milage ko or bhi behatar bana sakate hai
 So let's have a look at some such useful tips
 1
 There is a deep relationship between tire pressure pressure and the mileage of the vehicle
 aapaki car kaa tair pressure kaaphi had tak aapaki car ke milage par asar daalata he
 It is better to periodically check the tire pressure of your car
 khaskar jab lambii drive par ja rahe hon
 Also keep an eye on the grip of your tires
 agar tair ghis gaya ho to use turant badal den
 Do the tire pressure check twice a week in the morning
 2
 Drive the car with love Just like humans, vehicles also need love
 kabhi bhi raf drive na karen
 Use the clutch, gear, brake and accelerator to measure
 sahi vakt par gear badalen
 Never drive a clutch while driving
 3
 Avoid short-distance drives, as long as possible avoid short-distance drives
 aksar kam duuri kii drive main gaadi kii milage kam ho jaati he
 Due to repeated engine start and stop, the car does not give good mileage
 4
 Keep the glass closed while driving
 Aerodynamic is also related to the mileage of the vehicle
 gaadi chalaate vakt koshish karen ki gaadi ke saare shishe band hon
 If you open the glass and drive the car, it may be that your petrol tank empties quickly
 5
 Speed and gear synergy is essential Speed and gear synergy is very important for better mileage
 sahi speed par sahi gear lagaaein
 You can get good mileage by driving petrol car at 2000 rpm and diesel car at 1500 rpm
 6
 Keep the car light
 For better mileage, try to avoid unnecessary weight in your car while you are driving
 gaadi main sirf jarurat ke saamaan hi rakhen
 The lighter the vehicle, the better the mileage
 7
 Turn off the vehicle when not needed
 It is usually seen that many car drivers do not stop the engine of the vehicle when stuck in traffic or at traffic signals
 agar aapako trephic main ek minute se zyada ruknaa pade to apni car kaa ingine band kar den
 With this you will also save petrol and help in preventing pollution
 8
 Servicing the car at the right time It is also necessary to have servicing done at the right time for good mileage
 niyamit antaraal par apni car kii ingine oil, air filter, gear oil badalawaate rahen
 So that the engine of the car is not negatively affected
 9
 Use a root plan Always make a route plan before leaving on drive
 isse aap bevajaah idhar-udhar ghoomane se bachenge or eendhan bachegaa
 10
 sahi petrol pump kaa chunaav karengadi main petrol bharaane ke liye sahi petrol pump kaa chunaav karen jahaan tel main milawat naa kii jaati ho
 Also, keep in mind that petrol or diesel should always be filled in the morning

 If you have been given a check by someone and you deposit it in the bank to cash it, then it is important that the issuer of the check has at least as much money as the check he has issued
 agar uske khate main utane paise nahin hote hai to bank check ko dishonour kar detaa he
 This is called check bounce
 jab check bouns hota he, to bank kii ore se ek slip bhi di jaati he
 The reason for the check bounce is written in this slip
 agar check bouns ho jaataa he, to sabase pehle ek maheene ke andar check jari karne vaale ko legal notice bhejnaa hota he
 In this notice, it is said that the check he gave has bounced, now he should give the amount of the check to him within 15 days
 iske baad 15 din tak intjaar karnaa hota he yadi check dene vaala us paise kaa bhugtan 15 din main kar detaa he to maamla yaheen sulajh jaataa he
 Filed in civil court
 If the issuer of the check refuses to pay the money or does not respond to the legal notice, you can file a case in the civil court under section 138 of the Negotiable Instruments Act 1881
 iske tahat aaropee ko 2 saal kii sajaa or jurmaana donon ho saktaa he
 The amount of the fine can be double the amount of the check
 cese daayar karne ke baad aap court se apil kar sakate hai ki vah check jari karne vaale se check kii raashi kaa kuch hissaa shuruyaat main hi dilava de
 After this, the court usually gets 20 to 30 percent of the check amount in the beginning
 agar aap jeet jate hai, to court check jari karne vaale se paisa dilaa detaa he saath hi jo amount aapako shuruyaat main mila hua he, vah bhi aapke paas hi rahata he
 If you lose the case, the money you got at the beginning of the case has to be returned with interest
 criminal cese bhi kar sakate hai dairachek bouns ke maamle main aap bhartiya dand samhita yani ipisi kii dhara 420 ke tahat criminal cese bhi kar sakate hai
 This requires proving that the issuer of the check was dishonest
 iske liye aaropee ko 7 saal kii jail or jurmaana donon ho saktaa he
 Who can issue the check, tell you that a person can issue a check and the company can also issue it
 iske alaava trust or sosayadi samet anya sansthaaen bhi check jari kar sakati hai
 Along with this, let us also know that any check is valid for 3 months from the date of issue
 kab - kab check hota he bouns1
 If there is no money in the bank account of the check issuer
 2
 If there is less money in the check issuer's bank account than the amount written in the check
 3
 The check issuer has not corrected the signature

 party ne keemat main badhotaree waapas lene kii maang kii

 'didi' naam se mashhoor mamata ne apane samarthakon se mulya vruddhi vaapasi kii maang ko lekar rajya bhar main or reliyaan yojit karne ke liye kaha
